function isCTestActive(sTicketNumber)
{
    //noinspection UnreachableCodeJS
    return (
             null != window.ActiveCTests
             &amp;&amp; 'number' == typeof window.ActiveCTests[sTicketNumber]
             &amp;&amp; 1 === window.ActiveCTests[sTicketNumber]
           );
}

        return _.indexOf(activeFeatures, featureName) &gt; -1;
    }
})();
